Detailed Summary

## Introduction to USDT Perpetual Contracts

Perpetual contracts in the cryptocurrency world have been a game-changer, particularly with the advent of USDT (Tether) based contracts. These contracts allow traders to speculate on the price of cryptocurrencies without owning the underlying asset. But what exactly are [USDT Perpetual Contracts](https://learn.bybit.com/crypto/what-is-yield-farming/), and how do they work? This guide aims to demystify these financial instruments and provide a thorough understanding of their mechanics and implications for traders.

### What is USDT?

Before diving into the complexities of perpetual contracts, it's crucial to understand [USDT](https://learn.bybit.com/altcoins/what-is-usdt-a-beginners-guide-to-tether/), a stablecoin tied to the US dollar. This linkage to a stable fiat currency makes USDT a popular choice for traders looking to avoid the extreme volatility typical of cryptocurrencies like Bitcoin and Ethereum.
